        <script>
            function isStaticPage() {
                var path = window.location.pathname,
                    staticPaths = [
                        '/faq/',
                        '/privacy-policy/',
                        '/about-us/',
                        '/stories/',
                        '/terms/',
                        '/safety-issues/'
                    ];
        
                if(window.hasOwnProperty('fakeUrl') && window.fakeUrl === '/404/') {
                    return;
                }
        
                if( path !== '/' && !!staticPaths.join().match(path) ) {
                    window.fakeUrl = '/static/';
                }
        
            }
        
            isStaticPage();
        
        </script>
        
        
            <script>
                (function () {
                    var v = '?' + REVISION;
            
                    function loadScript(uri, cb) {
                        var s = document.createElement('script'),
                            counter = 0,
                            i = 0,
                            error;
            
                        if (uri instanceof Array) {
            
                            for (; i < uri.length; i++) {
            
                                loadScript(uri[i], function (err) {
            
                                    if (counter++ >= uri.length - 1 || err && !error) {
                                        cb && cb();
                                    }
            
                                    !error && err && (error = err);
                                });
            
                            }
            
                            return;
                        }
            
                        function src(s){
                            s.setAttribute('src', uri);
                            s.setAttribute('async', 'async');
                            s.async = true;
            
                            s.onload = function () {
                                cb();
                            };
            
                            s.onerror = cb;
            
                            document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(s);
                        }
            
                        src(s);
                    }
            
                    loadScript('/app/bundle.js' + v, function (err) {
            
                        if (err) {
            
                            loadScript(['/app/require.config.js' + v, '/app/packages/require.js' + v], function () {
                                require(['boot']);
                            });
            
                        }
            
                    });
                })();
            </script>
